<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Filed Pursuant to Rule 424(b)(5)<BR>Registration No. 333-221941 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><FONT COLOR="#ff4338"><B>Subject to Completion, dated June 20, 2018 </B></FONT></P>

December&nbsp;7, 2017) </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:3pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:15pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>$&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </B></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>$
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Floating Rate Notes Due 2020&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>$ &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Floating Rate Notes
Due 2021&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>$
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;% Notes Due
2020&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>$
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;% Notes Due
2021&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>$
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;% Notes Due
2023&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</B></P></DIV><DIV STYLE="position:relative;float:left; margin-left:3%; width:49%;padding-right:0%;padding-bottom:8pt;overflow:hidden;padding-top:3pt">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>$
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;% Notes Due 2025
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>$
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;% Notes Due 2028
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>$
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;% Notes Due 2038
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>$
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;% Notes Due 2048
</B></P></div><div style="clear:both; height:0pt; font-size:0pt">&nbsp;</div>
 <P STYLE="font-size:2pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P><center> <P STYLE="line-height:6.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:21%">&nbsp;</P></center>
<P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:3%; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Walmart Inc. is offering $&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; aggregate principal amount of our floating rate notes due 2020 (the
&#147;2020 floating rate notes&#148;), $&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; aggregate principal amount of our floating rate notes due 2021 (the &#147;2021 floating rate notes&#148; and, together with the 2020 floating rate notes, the
&#147;floating rate notes&#148;), $&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; aggregate principal amount of our &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;% notes due 2020 (the &#147;2020 fixed rate notes&#148;), $&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
aggregate principal amount of our &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;% notes due 2021 (the &#147;2021 fixed rate notes&#148;), $&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; aggregate principal amount of our &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;% notes due 2023 (the
&#147;2023 notes&#148;), $&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; aggregate principal amount of our &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;% notes due 2025 (the &#147;2025 notes&#148;), $&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; aggregate principal
amount of our &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;% notes due 2028 (the &#147;2028 notes&#148;), $&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; aggregate principal amount of our &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;% notes due 2038 (the &#147;2038 notes&#148;), and
$&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; aggregate principal amount of our &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;% notes due 2048 (the &#147;2048 notes&#148; and, together with the other fixed rate notes of each series, the &#147;fixed rate notes&#148;
and, collectively with the floating rate notes, the &#147;notes&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:3%; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We will pay interest on the 2020 floating rate notes on the
applicable dates specified herein, at a rate equal to the three-month London Interbank Offered Rate (&#147;LIBOR&#148;) plus/minus &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;basis points. We will pay interest on the 2021 floating rate notes on
the applicable dates specified herein, at a rate equal to three-month LIBOR plus/minus &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;basis points. We will pay interest on the fixed rate notes of each series on the applicable dates specified
herein, in each case, at the annual interest rate shown above for such series of notes. The notes of each series will mature on the dates specified herein. See &#147;Description of the Notes&#148; in this prospectus supplement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:3%; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Each series of fixed rate notes will be redeemable, as a whole or in part, at our option, as described under &#147;Description of the
Notes&#151;Optional Redemption of the Fixed Rate Notes&#148; in this prospectus supplement. None of the floating rate notes will be redeemable at our option. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:3%; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In May 2018, we entered into agreements (the &#147;Flipkart Agreements&#148;) with Flipkart Private Limited (&#147;Flipkart&#148;), the
Singapore holding company of the Flipkart group, a leading eCommerce business in India, and certain shareholders of Flipkart (the &#147;Flipkart Shareholders&#148;), pursuant to which we have agreed to acquire approximately 77 percent of the share
capital of Flipkart for an aggregate cash purchase price of approximately $16 billion (the &#147;Flipkart Acquisition&#148;). We intend to use a portion of the net proceeds from the sale of the notes to fund a portion of the purchase price for the
Flipkart Acquisition. The offering of the notes is not conditioned upon the consummation of the Flipkart Acquisition. However, if on or prior to June 7, 2019 (i)&nbsp;the Flipkart Acquisition has not closed, (ii)&nbsp;the Flipkart Agreements are
terminated, or (iii)&nbsp;we otherwise publicly announce that the Flipkart Acquisition will not be consummated, then we will be required to redeem all of the outstanding 2021 floating rate notes, 2021 fixed rate notes, 2023 notes, 2028 notes and
2038 notes (collectively, the &#147;Special Mandatory Redemption Notes&#148;) at a special mandatory redemption price equal to 101% of the aggregate principal amount of the Special Mandatory Redemption Notes of each series, plus accrued and unpaid
interest, if any, to, but not including, the date of redemption, as described under the heading &#147;Description of the Notes&#151;Special Mandatory Redemption&#148; in this prospectus supplement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:3%; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman">None of the 2020 floating rate notes, the 2020 fixed rate notes, the 2025 notes or the 2048 notes will be subject to the special mandatory
redemption, and the notes of each such series will remain outstanding even if we do not consummate the Flipkart Acquisition. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:3%; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The notes of
each series will be our senior unsecured debt obligations, will rank equally with our other senior unsecured indebtedness and will not be convertible or exchangeable. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:2pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:3%; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Investing in the notes involves certain risks. See &#147;<A HREF="#supp206936_6">Risk Factors</A>&#148; beginning on page S-7 of this
prospectus supplement. </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:2pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<div style ="BORDER-BOTTOM:1.00pt solid #000000;BORDER-LEFT:1.00pt solid #000000;BORDER-RIGHT:1.00pt solid #000000;BORDER-TOP:1.00pt solid #000000;MARGIN-LEFT:0px; MARGIN-RIGHT:0px;max-width:100%"><div style="width:97%; margin-top:1.5%; margin-left:1.5%; margin-right:-1.25%">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="supp206936_5"></A>SUMMARY </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>The following summary highlights information contained or incorporated by reference in this prospectus supplement and the accompanying
prospectus. It may not contain all of the information that you should consider before investing in the notes. You should carefully read this entire prospectus supplement, as well as the accompanying prospectus and the documents incorporated by
reference in this prospectus supplement and the accompanying prospectus. </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Walmart Inc. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Walmart Inc. is engaged in retail and wholesale operations in various formats around the world and is the world&#146;s largest retailer, with
total revenue of $500.3 billion and total net sales of $495.8 billion in our fiscal year ended January&nbsp;31, 2018. Through our operations, we help people around the world save money and live better&#151;anytime and anywhere&#151;in retail stores
and through eCommerce. Through innovation, we are striving to create a customer-centric experience that seamlessly integrates digital and physical shopping into an omni-channel offering that saves time for our customers. Physical retail encompasses
our brick and mortar presence in each of the markets in which we operate. eCommerce is comprised of our eCommerce websites, mobile commerce applications and transactions involving both an eCommerce platform and a physical format, which we refer to
as omni-channel. Each week, we serve nearly 270&nbsp;million customers who visit our more than 11,700&nbsp;stores and numerous eCommerce websites under 65 banners in 28 countries. Employing approximately 2.3&nbsp;million associates around the world,
we serve our customers and members primarily through the operation of three business segments: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Walmart U.S. is our largest segment with three primary store formats and eCommerce, as well as an omni-channel offering. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Walmart International consists of our operations outside of the U.S. and includes retail, wholesale, eCommerce and other businesses. These categories, other than eCommerce, consist of many formats, including
supercenters, supermarkets, hypermarkets, warehouse clubs (including Sam&#146;s Clubs) and cash&nbsp;&amp; carry. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Sam&#146;s Club consists of membership-only warehouse clubs in the U.S. and Puerto Rico, as well as eCommerce through samsclub.com. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We operate in all 50 states in the United States, Washington D.C. and Puerto Rico and, through wholly-owned subsidiaries, in Argentina,
Brazil, Canada, Chile, China, India, Japan and the United Kingdom. Through majority-owned subsidiaries, we operate in Africa (Botswana, Ghana, Kenya, Lesotho, Malawi, Mozambique, Namibia, Nigeria, South Africa, Swaziland, Tanzania, Uganda and
Zambia), Central America (Costa Rica, El Salvador, Guatemala, Honduras and Nicaragua), and Mexico. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Walmart Inc. was incorporated in the
State of Delaware on October&nbsp;31, 1969. We maintain our principal executive offices at 702 S.W. 8th Street, Bentonville, Arkansas 72716. Our main telephone number is
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">479-273-4000.</FONT></FONT> The address of our corporate website is at www.corporate.walmart.com. The information contained on our corporate website or any other website maintained by
us is not part of this prospectus supplement, the accompanying prospectus or the registration statement of which the accompanying prospectus is a part. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Recent Developments </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We have recently taken several strategic actions that we believe will further position our portfolio for long-term growth. Each of the
transactions summarized below remains subject to closing conditions, including the receipt of regulatory approvals: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">

<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">We have agreed to the combination of J Sainsbury plc and ASDA Group Limited (&#147;ASDA&#148;), our wholly owned United Kingdom retail subsidiary, in connection with which we would receive approximately 42 percent of
the share capital (initially representing 29.9 percent of the outstanding voting shares) of the combined business and approximately &pound;2.975 billion in cash, subject to customary closing adjustments, while we would retain the pre-closing
obligations under the ASDA defined benefit plan (the &#147;UK Combination&#148;). </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">We have agreed to sell 80 percent of Walmart Brazil to Advent International (&#147;Advent&#148;) for up to approximately $250 million in contingent consideration, and in which transaction, we will provide an
indemnification for certain pre-closing tax and legal contingencies (the &#147;Brazilian Divestiture&#148;). Additionally, Advent has agreed to contribute capital to the business over a three-year period following the closing of the Brazilian
Divestiture. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

announcement by the Company that the Flipkart Acquisition will not be consummated. See &#147;Description of the Notes&#151;Special Mandatory Redemption.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="supp206936_6"></A>RISK FACTORS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Investing in the notes involves certain risks. Before making a decision to invest in the notes, you should carefully consider all of the
information set forth in this prospectus supplement, the accompanying prospectus and the documents incorporated by reference into the this prospectus supplement and the accompanying prospectus and in any free writing prospectus relating to the
offering being made hereby or the notes that we file with the SEC. We discuss certain risks relating to our business in our Annual Report on Form 10-K under the heading &#147;Part I. Item&nbsp;1A. Risk Factors,&#148; which is incorporated by
reference in this prospectus supplement and the accompanying prospectus. See &#147;Where You Can Find More Information&#148; in this prospectus supplement and the accompanying prospectus. </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>We may be unable to consummate the Flipkart Acquisition, the UK Combination, the Brazilian Divestiture and/or our other announced divestitures, and the
impacts of those transactions that are consummated may be different from the impacts that we currently foresee for such transactions. </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">It is uncertain that any of our pending acquisition or divestiture transactions will be consummated in light of the conditions that must be
satisfied in order for each such transaction to be closed. If the Flipkart Acquisition is not consummated, we will not realize the benefits that we currently expect from such transaction. Alternatively, if the Flipkart Acquisition is consummated, we
may not realize any or all of the benefits that we currently expect from such transaction, we may need to make additional investments in the business in order for the business to develop in line with our expectations or we may find that any
indemnification payments made to us with respect to the Flipkart Acquisition are inadequate to make us whole for any losses or damages that we incur or suffer in connection with such transaction. We expect to record significant goodwill and
indefinite-lived intangible assets on our consolidated balance sheet if the Flipkart Acquisition is consummated. We assess the realizability of goodwill and indefinite-lived intangible assets annually and whenever events or changes in circumstances
indicate that these assets may be impaired. Our ability to realize the value of the goodwill and intangible assets will depend on the future cash flows of Flipkart. If we do not realize the value of the goodwill and intangible assets recorded on our
balance sheet upon the closing of the Flipkart Acquisition, we could recognize material non-cash charges relating to the impairment of those assets. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If the UK Combination, the Brazilian Divestiture and the divestitures of our banking operations in Walmart Canada and Walmart Chile are not
consummated, we may need to develop new strategies for the retained businesses, make additional investments in such businesses and may incur losses in respect of the Brazilian operations in future periods. If the UK Combination and the divestitures
of our banking operations in Walmart Canada and Walmart Chile are consummated, we will no longer have the cash flow generated by such businesses. The losses expected to be recognized in relation to the consummation of each of the UK Combination and
the Brazilian Divestiture may be greater than we currently expect. We may be liable for claims, including claims for indemnification, in relation to each of our divestiture transactions. With regard to the Brazilian Divestiture, we have agreed to
indemnify Advent in respect of pre-closing tax and legal contingencies and we may find ourselves liable for other claims. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>If we do not consummate
the Flipkart Acquisition on or prior to the Outside Date or the Flipkart Agreements are terminated on or prior to such date or we otherwise publicly announce that the Flipkart Acquisition will not be consummated, then we will be required to redeem
all of the Special Mandatory Redemption Notes then outstanding. </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The completion of the Flipkart Acquisition is subject to the
satisfaction or waiver of various conditions, some of which are beyond our control. Each of the Flipkart Agreements contains certain termination provisions permitting Walmart, on the one hand, and Flipkart or the Flipkart Shareholders, on the other
hand, to terminate the Flipkart Agreements under certain circumstances. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">S-7 </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If the Flipkart Acquisition has not been consummated on or prior to the Outside Date, if the
Flipkart Agreements are terminated on or prior to the Outside Date or if we otherwise publicly announce on or prior to the Outside Date that the Flipkart Acquisition will not be consummated, then we will be required to redeem all outstanding Special
Mandatory Redemption Notes on the special mandatory redemption date at a special mandatory redemption price equal to 101% of the aggregate principal amount of the Special Mandatory Notes, plus accrued and unpaid interest, if any, to, but excluding,
the special mandatory redemption date. See &#147;Description of the Notes&#151;Special Mandatory Redemption&#148; in this prospectus supplement. If we redeem the Special Mandatory Redemption Notes pursuant to the special mandatory redemption, you
may not obtain the return that you expected on your investment in the Special Mandatory Redemption Notes. Whether or not the special mandatory redemption is ultimately triggered, it may adversely affect trading prices for the Special Mandatory
Redemption Notes prior to the special mandatory redemption date. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Upon consummation of the Flipkart Acquisition (including under
circumstances in which we acquire less than 77 percent of the share capital of Flipkart and/or the Flipkart Agreements are amended or otherwise modified), you will have no rights under the special mandatory redemption provisions, nor will you have
any right to require us to repurchase your notes if, between the closing of this offering and the consummation of the Flipkart Acquisition, we experience any changes (including any material adverse changes) in our business or financial condition, or
if the terms of the Flipkart Agreements change, including in material respects. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">None of the 2020 floating rate notes, the 2020 fixed rate
notes, the 2025 notes or the 2048 notes will be subject to the special mandatory redemption, and the notes of each such series will remain outstanding even if we do not consummate the Flipkart Acquisition. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>We may be unable to redeem any or all of the Special Mandatory Redemption Notes in the event of a special mandatory redemption. </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We are not obligated to place the proceeds of the offering of any notes in escrow prior to the consummation of the Flipkart Acquisition or to
provide the holders of the Special Mandatory Redemption Notes a security interest in those proceeds, and the indenture governing the notes imposes no other restrictions on our use of these proceeds during this time. Accordingly, we will need to fund
any special mandatory redemption of the Special Mandatory Redemption Notes using the net proceeds of the sale of the notes that we have voluntarily retained and from other sources of liquidity. In the event of a special mandatory redemption, we may
not have sufficient cash on hand to redeem any or all of the Special Mandatory Redemption Notes of a series, which would constitute an event of default under the indenture as to the Special Mandatory Redemption Notes of such series and have material
adverse consequences for us and the holders of the notes. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Active trading markets for the notes of any or all series may not develop. </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The notes of each series are a new issue of securities with no established trading market. We do not intend to apply for listing of the notes
of any series on any securities exchange. We cannot assure you trading markets for the notes of any series will develop or of the ability of holders of the notes to sell their notes or of the prices at which holders may be able to sell their notes.
In the past, some of our debt securities have been thinly traded. Certain of the underwriters have advised us that they or certain of their respective affiliates may make a market in the notes of each series. However, none of the underwriters is
obligated to do so, and any market making activity with respect to the notes of any or all series by an underwriter may be discontinued by that underwriter, in its sole discretion, at any time and without notice. If no active trading markets develop
for the notes of a series, you may be unable to resell the notes of that series at any price or at their fair market value. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Rating agencies continually review the ratings they have assigned to companies and their debt securities. Negative changes in the ratings
assigned to us, notes of any series or our debt securities generally could have an adverse effect on the market prices of the notes of any series. The indenture that will govern the notes contains no limitation on the amount of long-term debt or
other indebtedness that we may incur. If our aggregate indebtedness is too substantial, one or more of the rating agencies that rate series of our outstanding long-term and short-term debt may downgrade the rating of our outstanding debt securities,
including the notes of one or more of the series of notes offered hereby. Such a downgrade in the rating of such notes could adversely affect the market for those notes and the yields on such notes. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>The indenture does not contain any financial covenants. </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Neither we nor any of our subsidiaries are restricted from incurring additional unsecured debt or other liabilities, including senior debt,
under the indenture governing the notes. If we incur additional debt or liabilities, our ability to pay our obligations on the notes could be adversely affected. We expect that we will from time to time incur additional debt and other liabilities.
In addition, the notes will not, and the indenture that will govern the notes does not, contain any provision restricting us from paying dividends or issuing or repurchasing our securities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The indenture under which the notes of all series will be issued contains no financial covenants of the Company, and our credit agreements
contain only limited covenants, which restrict our ability to grant liens to secure indebtedness and to effect mergers and sales of all or substantially all of our assets. As a result, you are not protected under the indenture in the event of a
highly leveraged transaction (such as the Flipkart Acquisition), reorganization, a default under our existing indebtedness, restructuring, merger or similar transaction that may adversely affect you, except to the extent described under
&#147;Description of the Debt Securities&#151;Provisions of the Indenture&#151;Amalgamation, Consolidation, Merger or Sale of Assets&#148; in the accompanying prospectus. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Uncertainty relating to the LIBOR calculation method and potential phasing out of LIBOR after 2021 may adversely affect the value of the floating rate
notes of each series offered hereby. </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The floating rate notes of each series offered hereby will bear interest at a rate based on
LIBOR. On July&nbsp;27, 2017, the U.K. Financial Conduct Authority (the &#147;FCA&#148;) announced that it will no longer persuade or compel banks to submit rates for the calculation of LIBOR rates after 2021. Actions by the FCA, other regulators or
law enforcement agencies may result in changes to the method by which LIBOR is calculated. At this time, it is not possible to predict the effect of any such changes or any other reforms to LIBOR that may be enacted in the United Kingdom or
elsewhere. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">S-9 </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The FCA&#146;s announcement indicates that the continuation of LIBOR on the current basis is
not guaranteed after 2021. It is not possible to predict the effect of the changes in LIBOR, or the substitution of another reference rate for LIBOR, any changes in the methods pursuant to which LIBOR rates are determined or any other reforms to
LIBOR that will be enacted in the United Kingdom and elsewhere, which may adversely affect the trading market for LIBOR-based securities, including the floating rate notes, or result in the phasing out of LIBOR as a reference rate for securities. In
addition, any changes announced by the FCA, the ICE Benchmark Administration Ltd. (the independent administrator of LIBOR) or any other successor governance or oversight body, or future changes adopted by such body, in the method pursuant to which
LIBOR rates are determined may result in a sudden or prolonged increase or decrease in reported LIBOR rates. If that were to occur, the level of interest payments under the floating rate notes outstanding at the time of any such event would be
affected, and the value of such floating rate notes may be materially affected. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Uncertainty as to the nature of such potential changes
may adversely affect the trading market for LIBOR-based securities, including the floating rate notes of each series offered hereby. If LIBOR is discontinued or is no longer quoted prior to the maturity date of the floating rate notes of each series
offered hereby and the calculation agent determines an Alternative Rate (as defined herein) for LIBOR, then the calculation agent may, after consultation with us, make certain Adjustments (as defined herein) to the Alternative Rate or the spread
thereon, as well as the business day convention, interest determination dates and related provisions and definitions, in each case that are consistent with industry-accepted practices for such Alternative Rate, which may result in interest payments
differing from those previously made with respect to the floating rate notes and could materially affect the value of the floating rate notes of each series. See &#147;Description of the Notes&#151;Interest Rate on the Floating Rate Notes.&#148;
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>The amount of interest payable on the floating rate notes is set only once per quarter based on the three-month LIBOR rate on the interest
determination date, which rate may fluctuate substantially. </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Historically, the level of the three-month LIBOR has experienced
significant fluctuations. You should note that historical levels, fluctuations and trends of the three-month LIBOR rate are not necessarily indicative of future levels, fluctuations and/or trends. Any historical upward or downward trend in the
three-month LIBOR rate is not an indication that the three-month LIBOR rate is more or less likely to increase or decrease at any time during a floating rate interest period, and you should not take the historical levels of the three-month LIBOR
rate as an indication of its future performance. You should further note that although the actual three-month LIBOR rate on an interest payment date or at other times during an interest period may be higher than the three-month LIBOR rate on the
applicable interest determination date, you will not benefit from the three-month LIBOR rate at any time other than on the interest determination date for such interest period. As a result, changes in the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">three-month</FONT> LIBOR rate occurring during any interest rate period for the floating rate notes may not result in a comparable change in the market value of the floating rate notes. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">S-10 </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="supp206936_7"></A>RECENT DEVELOPMENTS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We have recently taken several strategic actions that we believe will further position our portfolio for long-term growth, including entering
into agreements to effect the transactions described below. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Flipkart Acquisition </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:2%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>The Flipkart Agreements </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On May&nbsp;9, 2018, we entered into (i)&nbsp;a Share Issuance and Acquisition Agreement (the &#147;Share Issuance Agreement&#148;) with
Flipkart pursuant to which we will purchase from Flipkart ordinary shares in Flipkart (&#147;Ordinary Shares&#148;) for an aggregate purchase price of $2 billion in cash (the &#147;Share Issuance&#148;), and (ii)&nbsp;a Share Purchase Agreement (the
&#147;Share Purchase Agreement&#148;) with the Flipkart Shareholders pursuant to which we will purchase from the Flipkart Shareholders, contemporaneously with the closing of the Share Issuance, Ordinary Shares and preference shares in Flipkart
(&#147;Preference Shares&#148; and, together with the Ordinary Shares, the &#147;Flipkart Shares&#148;) for an aggregate purchase price of approximately $14 billion in cash (the &#147;Secondary Share Purchase&#148;). Upon completion of the Flipkart
Acquisition, all Preference Shares will convert into Ordinary Shares. As a result of the Flipkart Acquisition, we expect to acquire approximately 77 percent of the share capital of Flipkart for an aggregate purchase price of approximately $16
billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Upon completion of the Flipkart Acquisition, we will have the right to designate five individuals for appointment as members of
Flipkart&#146;s board of directors, two of which may not be affiliated with us and will have the right to cause the appointment of the chief executive officer and chief financial officer, among other senior officers, of Flipkart. Following
completion of the Flipkart Acquisition, Flipkart will become a consolidated subsidiary of Walmart Inc. and will be consolidated based on a December&nbsp;31 year-end with a one month lag. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pursuant to the Share Issuance Agreement, at any time during the period beginning on the closing date of the Flipkart Acquisition and ending
on the first anniversary thereof, we will have the right to purchase or allow other persons to purchase from Flipkart additional Ordinary Shares with an aggregate purchase price of up to $3&nbsp;billion. These additional Ordinary Shares will be
purchased for the same price per share as the Ordinary Shares issued in the Share Issuance, subject to adjustment for any stock splits, stock dividends or similar transactions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Flipkart Agreements contain representations and warranties and covenants of the parties customary for transactions of this nature. Closing
under the Flipkart Agreements is subject to the satisfaction or waiver of various conditions precedent, including, among others: the absence of a material adverse change in Flipkart&#146;s business; regulatory approval by the Competition Commission
of India; the accuracy of representations and warranties, and performance of covenants, in all material respects; the absence of governmental or shareholder litigation challenging the Flipkart Acquisition; and the contemporaneous closing of the
Share Issuance and Secondary Share Purchase. See &#147;Description of the Notes&#151;Special Mandatory Redemption&#148; below. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
Flipkart Agreements also contain customary termination rights for the parties, including, among others, termination by Walmart if the Flipkart Acquisition has not been consummated by March&nbsp;9, 2019 (subject to extension for 30 days in certain
circumstances). No termination fee would be payable by any party if the Flipkart Agreements are terminated. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:2%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>About Flipkart
</I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Flipkart Private Limited, the holding company of Flipkart group, is incorporated in Singapore and has direct and indirect
subsidiaries in India that are engaged in the business of operating in India online market places for e-commerce. Flipkart is one of the leading e-commerce players in India, especially for sales of electronics, large appliances, mobile and fashion
and apparel in India. We believe that Flipkart is well positioned to leverage its integrated ecosystem in India, which is defined by localized service, deep insights into Indian customers and a best-in-class supply chain. Flipkart&#146;s supply
chain arm, eKart, has approximately 850 delivery hubs, making approximately 500,000 deliveries daily. After completion of the Flipkart Acquisition, Walmart and Flipkart will </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">S-11 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
maintain distinct brands and operating structures. Currently, Walmart India operates 21&nbsp;Best Price cash-and-carry stores and one fulfillment center in 19 cities across nine states in India,
with more than 95 percent of sourcing coming from India. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For its fiscal year ended March&nbsp;31, 2018, Flipkart had gross merchandise
value, or GMV, of orders placed on its marketplace, without reduction for returns, of approximately $7.5 billion and recorded total revenue of approximately 301,644 million rupees, or approximately $4.6 billion, translated into U.S. dollars using an
exchange rate of <FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:9.5pt"><FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:ARIAL">&#8377;</FONT></FONT>64.935 = $1.00, as of March 31, 2018. If the Flipkart Acquisition were to close at the end of the second quarter of our
fiscal year ending January&nbsp;31, 2019, we anticipate that we would have a negative impact of approximately $0.25 to $0.30 per share on our fully diluted earnings per share for such fiscal year. In addition, we would expect that in our fiscal year
ending January&nbsp;31, 2020, the Flipkart operations would have a negative effect of approximately $0.60 per share on our fully diluted earnings per share for such fiscal year, including operating losses of approximately $0.40 to $0.45 per share,
assuming minimal tax benefits for losses in the near to mid-term, and including approximately $0.05 per share relating to amortization of intangible assets and depreciation of short-lived assets resulting from purchase accounting. In addition,
approximately $0.15 of such per share amount would arise from interest expense. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Sainbury&#146;s/ASDA Transaction </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:2%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>The UK Combination </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On April&nbsp;30, 2018, we and J Sainsbury plc (&#147;Sainbury&#146;s&#148;) announced a proposed combination of Sainbury&#146;s and ASDA, our
wholly owned United Kingdom retail subsidiary. Upon consummation of the UK Combination, we will hold approximately 42 percent of the share capital of the combined business (comprised of 29.9 percent of Sainsbury&#146;s ordinary shares, with full
voting rights attached, with the balance held as non-voting shares convertible in certain circumstances into voting shares) and such investment will be subject to certain standstill and lock-up provisions. Upon consummation of the U.K. Combination,
we will initially have the right to appoint two directors to the board of directors of the combined company, which is expected to be comprised of twelve directors. In addition, we will receive approximately &pound;2.975 billion in cash, subject to
customary closing adjustments. We will retain ASDA&#146;s obligations under the ASDA defined benefit plan. The obligation of Sainbury&#146;s and our obligation to consummate the UK Combination are subject to the satisfaction or waiver of certain
conditions precedent. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ASDA had net sales of approximately &pound;22.2 billion, or approximately $28.7 billion, for the year ended
December 31, 2017, translated into U.S. dollars using the weighted average monthly exchange rate for the year ended December 31, 2017 of &pound;0.7750 = $1.00. Sainsbury&#146;s had announced revenue for the 52 weeks to March 10, 2018, calculated in
accordance with International Financial Reporting Standards, of approximately &pound;28.5 billion. Following consummation of the UK Combination, our cash flows from the combined business will be derived solely from the cash dividends that we receive
in respect of the share capital that we hold in the combined business. We can provide no assurance as to the timing, frequency or amount of such dividends. Upon consummation of the UK Combination, we will deconsolidate the ASDA operations from our
financial statements and thereafter record our investment in the combined company as an equity method investment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The combination of
Sainbury&#146;s and ASDA would create one of the leading grocery, general merchandise and clothing retail groups in the United Kingdom. Following consummation of the UK Combination, both the Sainsbury&#146;s and ASDA brands will be maintained, but
the brands will be combined to create a complementary network of more than 2,800 stores and several of the UK&#146;s most visited retail websites, to create greater choice for customers through more store formats and channels. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As a result of the UK Combination, we expect to recognize a loss of approximately $2 billion based on the value of the Sainsbury&#146;s shares
to be received in the UK Combination and foreign exchange rates as of April&nbsp;30, 2018. Due to the conditions to complete the transaction, including regulatory approval, which could extend in the second half of calendar year 2019, the timing of
the loss recognition is not yet determined. The amount of the </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">S-12 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
loss we actually recognize with respect to the UK Combination could be significantly different from the estimate of such loss discussed above due to changes in the fair value of the
Sainsbury&#146;s shares to be received in the UK Combination and changes in currency exchange rates. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We expect the impact to earnings to
be slightly dilutive in the first full year following completion of the UK Combination and neutral to slightly accretive in subsequent years, as synergies are realized. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Divestiture of Brazilian Operations </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In
June 2018, we entered into an agreement with Advent International LLC (&#147;Advent&#148;) pursuant to which we agreed to sell to Advent 80 percent of the equity in our Brazilian retail operations. Under the terms of the agreement, we may receive up
to approximately $250 million in contingent consideration, and we will provide an indemnification for certain pre-closing tax and legal contingencies, as well as other matters. Additionally, Advent has agreed to contribute capital to the business
over a three-year period following the closing of the Brazilian Divestiture. The obligations of the parties to consummate the Brazilian Divestiture are subject to certain conditions precedent, including regulatory approval. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2017, our Brazilian operation had net sales of approximately R$25.2 billion, or approximately $7.9
billion, translated into U.S. dollars using a weighted average exchange rate for the year ended December 31, 2017 of R$3.1935 = $1.00. We expect to recognize a loss of approximately $4.5 billion as a result of the Brazilian Divestiture in the second
quarter of our fiscal 2019. A significant portion of the net loss we expect to recognize will result from the recognition of cumulative foreign currency translation losses, and the final loss could fluctuate significantly due to changes in currency
exchange rates up to the date of close. Upon the consummation of the Brazilian Divestiture, we will deconsolidate the Brazilian operations from our financial statements and thereafter record our investment as an equity method investment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Apart from the loss referred to above, following consummation of the Brazilian Divestiture, we expect no ongoing material impact to our
earnings per share in the current fiscal year and a slight positive impact to our earnings per share in the next fiscal year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Other Matters </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We have also entered into agreements pursuant to which we would divest our banking operations in Walmart Canada and Walmart Chile. Such actions
are consistent with our focus on core retail capabilities. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">S-13 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="supp206936_8"></A>USE OF PROCEEDS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We estimate that the net proceeds from the sale of the notes, after deducting the underwriting discounts and payment of transaction expenses,
will be approximately $&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;. We intend to use a portion of the net proceeds from the sale of the notes to fund a portion of the purchase price for the Flipkart Acquisition and, to
the extent that the net proceeds from the sale of the notes are not used for such purpose, for general corporate purposes, including the payment of the redemption price in connection with any redemption of the Special Mandatory Redemption Notes.
This offering is not conditioned on the consummation of the Flipkart Acquisition. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In the event that the Flipkart Acquisition is not
consummated on or prior to the Outside Date, if the Flipkart Agreements are terminated on or prior to the Outside Date or if we otherwise publicly announce on or prior to the Outside Date that the Flipkart Acquisition will not be consummated, then
we will be required to redeem all outstanding Special Mandatory Redemption Notes then outstanding. In such case, we may use a portion of the net proceeds from the sale of the notes to fund all or a portion of the payment of the special mandatory
redemption price to be paid as a result of the special mandatory redemption of the Special Mandatory Redemption Notes. See &#147;Description of the Notes&#151;Special Mandatory Redemption.&#148; </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">S-14 </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="supp206936_12"></A>DESCRIPTION OF THE NOTES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>The following description of the terms and conditions of the notes supplements the description of the more general terms and conditions of
Walmart&#146;s debt securities contained in the accompanying prospectus. </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The notes of each series will be issued under and pursuant
to the indenture dated as of July&nbsp;19, 2005, as supplemented, between us and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., as trustee. The 2020 floating rate notes, the 2021 floating rate notes, the 2020 fixed rate notes, the 2021 fixed rate
notes, the 2023 notes, the 2025 notes, the 2028 notes, the 2038 notes and the 2048 notes are each a separate series of notes under the indenture. The notes of each series will be issued in registered book-entry form without interest coupons in
minimum denominations of $2,000 and integral multiples of $1,000 in excess thereof. The notes of each series will constitute our senior unsecured debt obligations and will rank equally among themselves, with the notes of the other series being
offered hereby and with all of our other existing and future senior unsecured debt. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The 2020 floating rate notes and the 2020 fixed rate
notes will mature on&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; , 2020; the 2021 floating rate notes and the 2021 fixed rate notes will mature on&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ,
2021; the 2023 notes will mature on&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; , 2023; the 2025 notes will mature on&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; , 2025; the 2028 notes will
mature on&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; , 2028; the 2038 notes will mature on &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;, 2038; and the 2048 notes will mature
on&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; , 2048. Unless previously purchased and cancelled or, to the extent permitted or required by such series of notes, redeemed prior to maturity, we will repay the notes of each
series at 100% of their principal amount, together with accrued and unpaid interest thereon, at their maturity. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I></I>The 2020 floating
rate notes will be initially issued in an aggregate principal amount of $&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ; the 2021 floating rate notes will be initially issued in an aggregate principal amount of
$&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ; the 2020 fixed rate notes will be initially issued in an aggregate principal amount of $&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ; the 2021
fixed rate notes will be initially issued in an aggregate principal amount of $&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ; the 2023 notes will be initially issued in an aggregate principal amount of
$&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ; the 2025 notes will be initially issued in an aggregate principal amount of $&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ; the 2028 notes will be initially issued in an
aggregate principal amount of $&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ; the 2038 notes will be initially issued in an aggregate principal amount of
$&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ; and the 2048 notes will be initially issued in an aggregate principal amount of $&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;. We may, without
the consent of the holders of the notes of a series, create and issue additional notes of that series ranking equally with and otherwise similar in all respects to the notes of that series (except for the public offering price, initial interest
accrual date, initial interest payment date, and the issue date) so that those additional notes will be consolidated and form a single series with the other outstanding notes of that series that we are offering hereby; <I>provided</I>, <I>however,
</I>that any additional notes of a series issued that are not fungible with the outstanding notes of that series for U.S. federal income tax purposes will be issued under one or more separate CUSIP and ISIN numbers. No additional notes of a series
may be issued if an event of default under the indenture has occurred and is continuing.<I> </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Interest Rate on the Floating Rate Notes </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The 2020 floating rate notes will bear interest at a floating rate equal to three-month LIBOR (as defined under &#147;Description of the Debt
Securities&#151;Interest and Interest Rates&#151;Floating Rate Debt Securities&#148; in the accompanying prospectus) determined by the calculation agent for the relevant interest period plus/minus
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;basis points (&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; %). Interest will accrue on the 2020 floating rate notes
from&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; , 2018 and will be payable in arrears on
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;,&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ,&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
and&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; of each year. The initial interest payment date for the 2020 floating rate notes will be&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; , 2018. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The 2021 floating rate notes will bear interest at a floating rate equal to three-month LIBOR determined by the calculation agent for the
relevant interest period plus/minus &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;basis points (&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; %). Interest will accrue on the 2021 floating rate

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The rate of interest on the floating rate notes of each series will be reset on each interest payment date. If any interest reset date for the
floating rate notes is not a business day, that interest reset date will be postponed to the next succeeding business day, unless that day is in the next succeeding calendar month, in which case, the interest reset date will be the business day
immediately preceding the related interest payment date. The interest rate set for the floating rate notes of a series on a particular interest reset date will remain in effect during the three-month interest period commencing on that interest reset
date. Each interest period will be the period from and including the interest reset date (other than the initial interest period, which will commence on and include&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; , 2018) to
but excluding the next interest reset date or until the maturity date of the floating rate notes of such series, as the case may be. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
calculation agent will determine the interest rate applicable to the floating rate notes of each series on the applicable interest determination date, which will be the second London Business Day immediately preceding the interest reset date for the
notes of such series. The interest rate determined on an interest determination date will become effective on and as of the next interest reset date. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The initial interest rate determination date for the floating rate notes will

on&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; , 2018. &#147;London Business Day&#148; means any day on which dealings in deposits in U.S. dollars are transacted in the London interbank market. </P>

of such series, the calculating of accrued interest and the calculation agent will conform to the descriptions set forth under &#147;Description of the Debt Securities&#151;Interest and Interest Rates&#151;Floating Rate Debt Securities&#148; in the
accompanying prospectus. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Notwithstanding the description of the method by which the calculation agent will determine LIBOR for the
floating rate notes of each series, as set forth under &#147;Description of the Debt Securities&#151;Interest and Interest Rates&#151;Floating Rate Debt Securities&#148; in the accompanying prospectus, if we or the calculation agent determine that
LIBOR has been permanently discontinued, then the calculation agent will use, as a substitute for LIBOR and for each future interest determination date, the alternative reference rate (the &#147;Alternative Rate&#148;) selected by the central bank,
reserve bank, monetary authority or any similar institution (including any committee or working group thereof) that is consistent with accepted market practice. As part of such substitution, the calculation agent will, after consultation with us,
make such adjustments (&#147;Adjustments&#148;) to the Alternative Rate or the spread thereon, as well as the business day convention, interest determination dates and related provisions and definitions, in each case that are consistent with
accepted market practice for the use of such Alternative Rate for debt obligations such as the relevant series of floating rate notes. If the calculation agent determines, and following consultation with us, that there is no clear market consensus
as to whether any rate has replaced LIBOR in customary market usage, (i)&nbsp;The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A. shall have the right to resign as calculation agent in respect of the relevant series of floating rate notes and
(ii)&nbsp;we will appoint, in our sole discretion, a new calculation agent to replace The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., solely in its role as calculation agent in respect of the floating rate notes of each series, to determine the
Alternative </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In determining the present value of the Remaining Scheduled Payments, we will discount such payments to the redemption date on a semi-annual
basis (assuming a 360-day year consisting of twelve 30-day months) using a discount rate equal to the Applicable Treasury Rate plus, in the case of the 2020 fixed rate notes,
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;basis points, in the case of the 2021 fixed rate notes,&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; basis points, in the case of the 2023
notes,&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; basis points, in the case of the 2025&nbsp;notes,&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; basis points, in the case of the 2028 notes,
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; basis points, in the case of the 2038 notes, &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; basis points, and in the case of the 2048 notes,
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; basis points. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The term &#147;Applicable Treasury Rate&#148;
means, with respect to any redemption date, the rate per annum equal to the semi-annual equivalent yield to maturity of the Comparable Treasury Issue. In determining this rate, we will assume a price for the Comparable Treasury Issue (expressed as a
percentage of its principal amount) equal to the Comparable Treasury Price for such redemption date. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The term &#147;Comparable Treasury
Issue&#148; means the United States Treasury security selected by an Independent Investment Banker as having a maturity comparable to the remaining term of the fixed rate notes of a series to be redeemed that would be utilized, at the time of
selection and in accordance with customary financial practice, in pricing a new issue of corporate debt securities of comparable maturity to the remaining term of the fixed rate notes of such series. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I></I>The term &#147;Independent Investment Banker&#148; means each of Barclays Capital Inc., Citigroup Global Markets Inc. and J.P. Morgan
Securities LLC and their respective successors as may be appointed from time to time by us; <I>provided</I>, <I>however</I>, that if any of the foregoing firms shall cease to be a primary U.S. Government securities dealer (a &#147;Primary Treasury
Dealer&#148;), we will substitute another Primary Treasury Dealer for such firm.<I> </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The term &#147;Comparable Treasury Price&#148;
means, with respect to any redemption date, the arithmetic average, as determined by the Independent Investment Banker, of the Reference Treasury Dealer Quotations for such redemption date. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The term &#147;Reference Treasury Dealer Quotations&#148; means, with respect to each Reference Treasury Dealer and any redemption date, the
arithmetic average, as determined by the Independent Investment Banker, of the bid and asked prices for the Comparable Treasury Issue (expressed in each case as a percentage of its principal amount) quoted in writing to the Independent Investment
Banker by such Reference Treasury Dealer by 5:00&nbsp;p.m., New York City time, on the third business day preceding such redemption date. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I></I>The term &#147;Reference Treasury Dealer&#148; means each of Barclays Capital Inc., Citigroup Global Markets Inc. and J.P. Morgan
Securities LLC and their respective successors; <I>provided</I>, <I>however</I>, that if any of the foregoing firms shall cease to be a Primary Treasury Dealer, we will substitute another Primary Treasury Dealer for such firm.<I> </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I></I>The term &#147;Remaining Scheduled Payments&#148; means, with respect to any fixed rate note, the remaining scheduled payments of the
principal thereof to be redeemed and interest thereon that would be due after the related redemption date but for such redemption; <I>provided</I>, <I>however</I>, that, if such redemption date is not an interest payment date with respect to such
note, the amount of the next scheduled interest payment thereon will be reduced by the amount of interest accrued thereon to such redemption date.<I> </I></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Flipkart Agreements also contain customary termination rights for the parties, including, termination by either party if the Flipkart
Acquisition has not been consummated by March&nbsp;9, 2019 (the &#147;End Date&#148;). Additionally, each of the Flipkart Agreements may be terminated on or prior to the End Date (i)&nbsp;by written mutual consent of the parties thereto,
(ii)&nbsp;by either party thereto if the conditions precedent to closing have not been satisfied or waived on or prior to the End Date, (iii)&nbsp;by any party thereto if a court or governmental entity in India, Singapore or the United States issues
an order enjoining the Share Issuance or the Secondary Share Purchase, or if the Share Issuance or the Secondary Share Purchase would otherwise be illegal in India, Singapore or the United States, (iv)&nbsp;by either party thereto, if the other
party is in breach of a representation, warranty or covenant and the breaching party has not cured the breach within 30 days; and (v)&nbsp;by Walmart if the other Flipkart Agreement has been terminated. No termination fee would be payable by any
party if the Flipkart Agreements are terminated. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The &#147;special mandatory redemption date&#148; means the 20th day (or if such day is
not a business day, the first business day thereafter) after the earliest to occur of (i)&nbsp;the Outside Date, if the Flipkart Acquisition has not been consummated on or prior thereto, (ii)&nbsp;the date of termination of the Flipkart Agreements,
or (iii)&nbsp;the date of public announcement by the Company that the Flipkart Acquisition will not be consummated. The Outside Date has been set at a date following the End Date so as to provide the parties to the Flipkart Agreements with the
flexibility to extend the End Date under the Flipkart Agreements, if circumstances so require. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Notwithstanding the foregoing,
installments of interest on the Special Mandatory Redemption Notes that are due and payable on interest payment dates falling on or prior to the special mandatory redemption date will be payable on such interest payment dates to the registered
holders as of the close of business on the relevant record dates in accordance with the terms of the Special Mandatory Redemption Notes and the indenture. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We will cause the notice of special mandatory redemption to be transmitted, with a copy to the trustee, within five business days after the
occurrence of the event triggering the special mandatory redemption to each holder at its registered address. If funds sufficient to pay the special mandatory redemption price of the outstanding Special Mandatory Redemption Notes of each series to
be redeemed on the special mandatory redemption date (plus accrued and unpaid interest, if any, to, but excluding, such date) are deposited with the trustee on or before such special mandatory redemption date, and certain other conditions are
satisfied, on and after such special mandatory redemption date, the outstanding Special Mandatory Redemption Notes will cease to bear interest. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">None of the 2020 floating rate notes, the 2020 fixed rate notes, the 2025 notes or the 2048 notes will be subject to the special mandatory
redemption, and the notes of each such series will remain outstanding even if we do not consummate the Flipkart Acquisition. </P>
